## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Unverified
    Unverified --> ModalOpen: Click Verify Button
    ModalOpen --> AssetLocationSelected: Select Yes/No
    AssetLocationSelected --> DistanceRequired: Select No
    AssetLocationSelected --> ReadyToSave: Select Yes
    DistanceRequired --> ReadyToSave: Select Distance
    ReadyToSave --> Saving: Click Save
    Saving --> ModalClosed: Success
    Saving --> ShowError: Error
    ShowError --> AssetLocationSelected: Retry
    ModalClosed --> Verified
    ModalOpen --> ModalClosed: Click Cancel
    Verified --> [*]
    
    note right of Unverified
        Initial state with
        Verify button visible
    end note
    
    note right of DistanceRequired
        If asset not at expected location,
        distance selection required
    end note
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([groupCoords function called])
    Start --> Init[Initialize result array and prev object]
    Init --> Loop{For each coordinate in array}
    Loop --> CheckPrev{Does prev exist with<br/>matching lat/long?}
    CheckPrev -->|Yes| AddToGroup[Add ID to last result groupedIds<br/>Update start time]
    CheckPrev -->|No| CreateNew[Create new coordinate object<br/>with groupedIds, start, end times]
    CreateNew --> AddToResult[Add to result array<br/>Update prev reference]
    AddToGroup --> NextItem{More items?}
    AddToResult --> NextItem
    NextItem -->|Yes| Loop
    NextItem -->|No| Return([Return grouped result array])
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant CoordinatesTable
    participant VerifyCell
    participant Modal
    participant API
    
    User->>CoordinatesTable: Load coordinates
    CoordinatesTable->>CoordinatesTable: Sort by time descending
    CoordinatesTable->>CoordinatesTable: Group by date
    CoordinatesTable->>CoordinatesTable: groupCoords()
    CoordinatesTable->>VerifyCell: Render cell
    
    User->>VerifyCell: Click Verify button
    VerifyCell->>Modal: Show modal (setShowModal true)
    Modal->>User: Display form
    
    User->>Modal: Select asset location (Yes/No)
    Modal->>VerifyCell: Update isAssetLocationExpected
    
    alt Asset not at expected location
        User->>Modal: Select distance off
        Modal->>VerifyCell: Update distanceOff
    end
    
    User->>Modal: Click Save
    VerifyCell->>API: updateEntityPositionUpdate (for each ID)
    
    alt Success
        API-->>VerifyCell: Success response
        VerifyCell->>Modal: Hide modal
        Modal-->>User: Close
    else Error
        API-->>VerifyCell: Error response
        VerifyCell->>Modal: Display error alert
        Modal-->>User: Show error message
    end
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[User clicks row] --> B[onRowClick called]
    B --> C[Extract lat, long, time]
    C --> D{elevationUnits<br/>== floor?}
    D -->|Yes| E[Get floor from references]
    D -->|No| F[floor = null]
    E --> G[Parse confidence radius]
    F --> G
    G --> H{radius valid?}
    H -->|No| I[radius = 0]
    H -->|Yes| J[Keep radius value]
    I --> K[addCoordinate]
    J --> K
    K --> L[Update map with<br/>SELECTED_COORDINATE]
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
graph TD
    A[coords array] --> B[orderBy time desc]
    B --> C[groupBy date]
    C --> D[Iterate dates]
    D --> E{Row expanded?}
    E -->|No| F[Show collapsed date row]
    E -->|Yes| G[groupCoords]
    G --> H[Map grouped coords to rows]
    H --> I{showIconColumn?}
    I -->|Yes| J[Render icon]
    I -->|No| K[Skip icon]
    J --> L[Render time cells]
    K --> L
    L --> M[Render lat/long]
    M --> N{showVerifyColumn?}
    N -->|Yes| O[Render VerifyCell]
    N -->|No| P[Skip verify]
    O --> Q[Complete row]
    P --> Q
    F --> R[All rows assembled]
    Q --> R
    R --> S[Pass to DetailsTable]
```
